 police ne na sirf apane apharan kii sajeesh rachane vaale vyakti ko giraftaar kar liya he, balki ab usee ke khilaaf jaanch shuru kar di he
 In fact, Udayraj, a resident of Gama-2 sector of Kasna police station area, was a real estate businessman, but due to GST and demonetization, he was buried in huge debt
 karjadaaron ke changul se bachane ke liye usne khud apane apharan kii sajeesh rach daali or ghar chhodkar bhaag gaya
 Not only this, at the behest of Udayraj, his son Aditya Kumar lodged a complaint of kidnapping of his father and made him the accused of giving loans
 police ke mutabik, udayraj par 60 lakh rupee kaa karj he
 But when the police discovered the kidnapped on Sunday, the whole story changed
 jo sachai saamne ai use jaanakar police stabdh rah gai
 On 9 March, Aditya lodged a complaint with the Kasna police station that his father had been kidnapped
 aditya ne bataaya ki uske pita bank main 3
 He had been kidnapped when he went to collect Rs 85 lakh
 isamen jarcha thana kshetra ke cholas gaanv nivasee abbaas, mujbbir or raja naam ke vyaktiyon ko namjad karaayaa gaya tha
 Noida DIG Luv Kumar said that after writing the report, the team led by Brijesh Kumar Verma, in-charge of Kasna police station, started investigating the incident
 or aakhirkaar servilans kii madad se police ne udayraj ko honda chowk ke kasana puliya se baraamad kar liya
 2 near Udayaraj
 90 lakh rupee bhi baraamad kiye gaye hai
 According to the information, Udayraj works as a property
 notebandi or jiestike baad uskaa kaam bilkul thap ho gaya
 Due to lack of business, he got into debt
 us par 60 lakh rupee kaa karj ho gaya
 Due to lack of work, he was unable to repay the loan, which made him very mentally disturbed
 udayraj ne bataaya kii ghar chhodane ke baad vah deyari ke dhandhe kii sambhaavnaaen talashne ke liye kai jagah gaya, jisase vah kamai kar karj chukaa sake
 Luv Kumar told that during interrogation Udayraj told that he has a loan of 60 lakh rupees, due to which he used to be very upset
 beeti 5 march ko usne apni patni ke liye ek patr likhakar ghar chhod diya tha
 The inquiry also revealed that Udayaraj was given a loan by Abbas, Muzabir and Raja, so he was named in a false incident of kidnapping, so that he could get freedom from debt
 pulipub is baat kii jaanch kar rahi he ki udayraj ne jo patr apni patni ko diya tha, usamen kya likhaa tha or us patr ke bare main parivaar waalon ne police ko jaankaree kyon nahin di
 He said that if any criminal conspiracy was found in the investigation, action would be taken against Udayraj and his family members

 - input IANS The 17-year-old girl's death game, the suicide game 'blue Whale', turned out to be the mastermind
 russian police ne masco se aaropee ladki ko giraftaar kar liya he
 She is a student of psychology and has confessed her crime to the police
 russian police ne aaropee ladki ko giraftaar kar court main pesh kiya, jahaan se use teen saal ke liye jail bhej diya gaya he
 Police said she used to threaten her victim that she would kill him and his family if he did not complete the 'blue Whale' task
 police ne aage kaha, vah is game ke jariye unheen logon ko apana shikaar banaati thi, jo log kisi tarah ke tanaav se jujh rahe hote the yaa phir tanaav se jude kaarnon ke chalate aatmahatya karne ke bare main soch rahe hote the
 Police is questioning the friends and family of the accused girl
 kya hota he 'blue whale' gemsaal 2013 main rus kephilip budekinnaam ke shaks ne 'blue whale' game banaaya tha
 This is a challenge in which you have to complete many tasks given by the group administrator within 50 days
 har task puraa hone par player ko apane haath par ek cat lagane ke liye kaha jaataa he
 The image that emerges in the last after completing the task is like a whale fish
 maut kaa khel he ye gemis game main sin in karne ke baad 50 dinon ke andar task puraa karne kii chunauti milti he
 This includes challenges such as harming yourself, watching horror movies in private, and tattooing the size of a whale fish on your arm
 is game kaa sabase khaufnak or aakhri task 50wein din diya jaataa he, jisamen khud ko jaan se maarane kii chunauti milti he
 Code F57 is written with a blade on the hand
 The administrator of this game keeps in constant contact with the game-player through Skype
 game khilne vaale ko har din ek code number diya jaataa he
 In this, writing the F57 with the blade on the hand is asked to upload its photo
 game kaa vinar use hi ghoshit kiya jaataa he, jo 50wein din apni jaan de detaa he
 So far, the children of 130 people are getting caught in the trap by understanding the game
 soshal mediaper 'blue whale' ap ko talasha ja rahaa he, lekin asal main yah na to game he or na hi ap he
 It is a trap of criminals
 media reports kii maane to is game kii vajah se duniya bhar main ab tak 130 logon kii jaan ja chuki he

 Jai Mata Di is being echoed everywhere in the Navratri, the whole country is immersed in the devotion of Mother
 madhya pradesh ke sihor salkanpur main viraaji maa vijayasana bhavy rup main darshan dekar bhakton kaa har dukh har leti hai
 After traveling 14 hundred stairs, the devotees reach the court of Mother and find a solution to their every sorrow
 maa ke is darbar main bhakt kii koi pukaar kabhi ansuni nahin rahati, raja ho yaa rank, maa sabhi par ek samaan krupa barsaati hai
 As the rising steps of the devotees touch the periphery of this dham, the whole body is filled with the power of Goddess Bhagwati, because this is the place where Mother Vijayasan is sitting on the beautiful mountain in its ultimate divine form
 jagat janani kaa ye wo dham he jo jagat bhar main salkanpur vaali maa vijayasana ke naam se prasiddh he
 In Salkanpur, this self-proclaimed idol of Viraji Siddheshwari Maa Vijayasan is that of Mata Parvati, who is seated with Lord Ganesha in her lap with an eagerness
 isi mandir main mahalakshmi, mahasaraswati or bhagwaan bhairav bhi virajman hai yani is ek mandir main kai devi-devataaon ke aashirwad kaa saubhaahgya bhakton ko praapt hota he
 According to the Puranas, Goddess Vijayasan is the incarnation of Goddess Parvati, who, on the insistence of the gods, killed the demon named Raktabija and protected the entire creation
 devi vijayasana ko kai bhakt kul devi ke rup main puujate hai
 Mother, where on the one hand, blesses virgins with a desired life partner
 vahiin santan kaa vardaan dekar bhakton kii suuni god bhar detii hai
 That is why the importance of this Dham of Goddess is not less than any Shaktipeeth

 udhar, india against karpshan (iasi) ke kaaryakarta arvind kejariwal ne chetavanee di thi ki aseem ko yadi reeha nahin kiya gaya to jail ke baahar hi dharna-pradarshan par baith jaaenge
 Meanwhile, Maharashtra Navnirman Sena chief Raj Thackeray has also supported Aseem, a resident of Uttar Pradesh
 mukhya nyaayadhish nyaayamurti mohit shah evam nyaayamurti nitin jamdar kii khandpeeth ne adhivaktaa sanskaar marathi dwaara daayar janhit yachika par sunwaayee karte hue aseem ko jamaanat de di
 India Against Corruption (IAC) activist Preeti Menon said that Aseem got bail on a bond of five thousand rupees
 iasi ke mayank gandhi ne bataaya ki aseem ne mumbai police dwaara unke khilaaf lagaae gaye deshadroh ke aaropon ko waapas lene tak jail se baahar aane se inkaar kiya he
 Home Minister RR Patil had said that the police and law department would be asked for an opinion on the treason charge leveled against Aseem
 iske kuch hi ghante baad cartoonist ne jail se baahar aane se inkaar kiya
 Kejriwal had earlier said, "release Aseem or arrest us
 " unhone kaha, "aseem ne bhrashtachar ke khilaaf or lokapal ke liye ladaai ladi he lekin unhen deshadrohi qaraar diya gaya he or jinhone koyale kii chori kii unhen deshbhakt kaha ja rahaa he
 " kejariwal ne kaha ki patil, soochna or prasaaran mantri ambika soni or congress pravaktaa manish tiwari ne sweekaar kiya he ki trivedi ke khilaaf upyukt maamla nahin banaaya gaya
 Patil had earlier admitted that the Ministry of Home Affairs had no role in the case against Trivedi and also assured that he would try to release her soon
 raaj ne aseem ke khilaaf deshadroh kaa maamla waapas lene evam unhen reeha karne kii maang kii
 As a cartoonist, Raj said that Aseem has only vented his anger through cartoons
 unhone kaha, "cartoon ke dwaara apni bhavanaaen vyakt karne main kya kharabi he
 "raj questioned why the hanging of Afzal Guru and Ajmal Kasab is delayed and the cartoonist has to face treason

 ) August 8 is important in the history of the country and the world for many reasons, all of which are prominent
 
 
 
 1549: France declares war against England
 1700: denmark or sweden ke bich shanti sandhi par hastakshar
 1919: Britain approves independence of Afghanistan in Rawalpindi Sandhi
 1942: mahatma gandhi ne bharat chodo andolan kii shuruyaat kii
 1945: Soviet Union declares war against Japan in World War II
 1988: 9 saal ke lambey yuddh ke baad roosi sena kii vaapasi afghanistan se shuru hui
